 What is Elasticity? What is an elasticity pratyasthata kii seemaa kya hoti he? chaliye jaanate he pratyasthata kii paribhaasha, gun or anekon chijen:pratyasthata (elasticity):pratyasthata padaarth kaa vah gun he, jiske kaaran vastu, us par lagaae gaye bahari bal se utpann kisi bhi prakaar ke parivartan kaa virodh karti he tathaa jaise hi bal hataa liya jaataa he, vah apni purv avasthaa main waapas aa jaati he
 Elastic limit: The limit of the magnitude of the inverse force through which the force of elasticity is retained in the material by applying less force and thereby eliminating the elasticity of the substance by applying more force is called the limit of elasticity
 vikruti (strain):kisi taar par virupak bal lagane par uski praanrabhik lambaai l main vruddhi l hoti he, to l / l kii vikti kehete he
 Stress: The force exerted on each unit area is called stress
 praratyasthata kaa yang mapank (young 's modulus of elasticity): pratibal or vikruti ke anupaat ko taar ke padaarth kii pratyasthata kaa yang mapank kehete hai
 Hooke's law: The deformation produced at a point in the range of elasticity is proportional to the stress applied to it
 yani ki pratibal x vikruti yaa , pratibal / vikruti = e (ek niyatank) = pratyasthata kaa gunankpratyasthata gunank (E) kaa maan bhinn-bhinn hota he
 Its s
 I
 The unit is Newton meter ^ -2
 jise pascal kehete hai

 supreme court centre sarkaar or paryaavaran mantralay kii laaparvaahiyon se naaraaz he
 The latest case relates to a report, which the Ministry of Environment was to present before the Supreme Court
